//===== TERMUXFILE: test/llamafile_proxy.py =====
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
ENHANCED PROXY - Executes commands in Termux properly via file queue
Works around Android sandbox limitations
"""
from http.server import HTTPServer, BaseHTTPRequestHandler
import json
import requests
import subprocess
import os
import time
from pathlib import Path

LLAMAFILE_URL = "http://127.0.0.1:8080"
PORT = 8888

# Command queue directory
QUEUE_DIR = Path.home() / ".jarvis_queue"
QUEUE_DIR.mkdir(exist_ok=True)

class EnhancedProxyHandler(BaseHTTPRequestHandler):
    def log_message(self, format, *args):
        print(f"[{self.log_date_time_string()}] {format % args}")
    
    def send_json(self, code, data):
        response = json.dumps(data, indent=2).encode()
        self.send_response(code)
        self.send_header('Content-Type', 'application/json')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*')
        self.end_headers()
        self.wfile.write(response)
    
    def do_OPTIONS(self):
        self.send_response(200)
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Methods', 'GET, POST')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Headers', 'Content-Type')
        self.end_headers()
    
    def do_GET(self):
        if self.path == '/health':
            try:
                response = requests.get(f"{LLAMAFILE_URL}/health", timeout=2)
                if response.status_code == 200:
                    self.send_json(200, {
                        "status": "healthy",
                        "model": "Qwen2.5-Coder-3B",
                        "backend": "llamafile",
                        "executor": "enhanced"
                    })
                else:
                    self.send_json(503, {"status": "unhealthy"})
            except:
                self.send_json(503, {"status": "unhealthy"})
        else:
            self.send_json(404, {"error": "Not found"})
    
    def do_POST(self):
        try:
            content_length = int(self.headers['Content-Length'])
            body = self.rfile.read(content_length)
            data = json.loads(body.decode())
            
            # ======= CHAT ENDPOINT =======
            if self.path == '/chat_sync':
                query = data.get('query', '').strip()
                if not query:
                    self.send_json(400, {"error": "Missing query"})
                    return
                
                print(f"\n[CHAT] {query}")
                
                response = requests.post(
                    f"{LLAMAFILE_URL}/v1/chat/completions",
                    json={
                        "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": query}],
                        "max_tokens": 100,
                        "temperature": 0.7
                    },
                    timeout=30
                )
                
                if response.status_code != 200:
                    self.send_json(500, {"success": False, "error": "LLM error"})
                    return
                
                result = response.json()
                text = result['choices'][0]['message']['content']
                print(f"[RESPONSE] {text}")
                
                self.send_json(200, {"success": True, "response": text})
            
            # ======= COMMAND GENERATION =======
            elif self.path == '/generate_sync':
                query = data.get('query', '').strip()
                if not query:
                    self.send_json(400, {"error": "Missing query"})
                    return
                
                print(f"\n[GENERATE] {query}")
                
                prompt = f"""Generate a Termux/Android shell command for: {query}

Requirements:
- Single line command only
- Use Termux-compatible syntax
- No placeholders or variables
- Use termux-* commands when appropriate (termux-notification, termux-toast, etc.)
- Output ONLY the command

Command:"""
                
                response = requests.post(
                    f"{LLAMAFILE_URL}/v1/chat/completions",
                    json={
                        "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
                        "max_tokens": 50,
                        "temperature": 0.3,
                        "stop": ["\n"]
                    },
                    timeout=30
                )
                
                if response.status_code != 200:
                    self.send_json(500, {"success": False, "error": "LLM error"})
                    return
                
                result = response.json()
                command = result['choices'][0]['message']['content'].strip().strip('`"\'')
                
                print(f"[COMMAND] {command}")
                
                self.send_json(200, {
                    "success": True,
                    "command": command,
                    "response": command
                })
            
            # ======= ENHANCED COMMAND EXECUTION =======
            elif self.path == '/execute':
                command = data.get('command', '').strip()
                if not command:
                    self.send_json(400, {"error": "Missing command"})
                    return
                
                print(f"\n[EXECUTE] {command}")
                
                # Try multiple execution methods
                
                # Method 1: Direct execution (works for simple commands)
                try:
                    result = subprocess.run(
                        command,
                        shell=True,
                        capture_output=True,
                        text=True,
                        timeout=30,
                        cwd=str(Path.home())  # Execute in home directory
                    )
                    
                    output = result.stdout + result.stderr
                    success = result.returncode == 0
                    
                    print(f"[EXIT CODE] {result.returncode}")
                    if output:
                        print(f"[OUTPUT] {output[:200]}")
                    
                    self.send_json(200, {
                        "success": success,
                        "output": output if output else "Command executed successfully (no output)",
                        "exit_code": result.returncode,
                        "method": "direct"
                    })
                    
                except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
                    # Method 2: Queue for background execution
                    cmd_id = int(time.time() * 1000)
                    cmd_file = QUEUE_DIR / f"cmd_{cmd_id}.sh"
                    result_file = QUEUE_DIR / f"result_{cmd_id}.txt"
                    
                    # Write command to queue
                    cmd_file.write_text(f"""#!/bin/bash
cd ~
{command} > {result_file} 2>&1
echo "EXIT_CODE=$?" >> {result_file}
""")
                    cmd_file.chmod(0o755)
                    
                    # Execute in background
                    subprocess.Popen([str(cmd_file)], start_new_session=True)
                    
                    self.send_json(200, {
                        "success": True,
                        "output": f"Command queued for execution (ID: {cmd_id})\nCheck {result_file} for results",
                        "exit_code": 0,
                        "method": "queued",
                        "result_file": str(result_file)
                    })
                    
                except Exception as e:
                    print(f"[ERROR] {e}")
                    self.send_json(500, {
                        "success": False,
                        "error": f"Execution failed: {e}\n\nTip: For complex commands, use Termux directly.",
                        "exit_code": -1
                    })
            
            else:
                self.send_json(404, {"error": "Endpoint not found"})
                
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[ERROR] {e}")
            import traceback
            traceback.print_exc()
            self.send_json(500, {"error": str(e)})

if __name__ == '__main__':
    print("="*70)
    print("ENHANCED JARVIS PROXY SERVER")
    print("="*70)
    print(f"Port: {PORT}")
    print(f"Backend: {LLAMAFILE_URL}")
    print(f"Queue: {QUEUE_DIR}")
    print()
    print("Features:")
    print("  ✅ Direct command execution")
    print("  ✅ Background queue for long commands")
    print("  ✅ Proper working directory (~)")
    print("  ✅ Termux-API compatible")
    print()
    print("Endpoints:")
    print("  GET  /health")
    print("  POST /chat_sync")
    print("  POST /generate_sync")
    print("  POST /execute")
    print("="*70)
    print()
    
    server = HTTPServer(('0.0.0.0', PORT), EnhancedProxyHandler)
    
    try:
        server.serve_forever()
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        print("\n🛑 Shutting down...")
        server.shutdown()


//===== TERMUXFILE: test/llamafile_proxy_lan.py =====
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
ENHANCED JARVIS PROXY - Now with LAN pairing support!
Compatible with JARVIS Android app LAN client pairing
"""
from http.server import HTTPServer, BaseHTTPRequestHandler
import json
import requests
import subprocess
import os
import time
import secrets
import hashlib
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime

LLAMAFILE_URL = "http://127.0.0.1:8080"
PORT = 8889

# Command queue directory
QUEUE_DIR = Path.home() / ".jarvis_queue"
QUEUE_DIR.mkdir(exist_ok=True)

# Security: Pairing and device management
DEVICES_FILE = Path.home() / ".jarvis_devices.json"
pairing_enabled = False
pairing_expiry = 0
devices = {}

def load_devices():
    global devices
    if DEVICES_FILE.exists():
        try:
            devices = json.loads(DEVICES_FILE.read_text())
        except:
            devices = {}

def save_devices():
    DEVICES_FILE.write_text(json.dumps(devices, indent=2))

def hash_token(token):
    return hashlib.sha256(token.encode()).hexdigest()

def generate_token():
    return secrets.token_hex(32)

def generate_device_id():
    return f"dev_{int(time.time())}_{secrets.randbelow(9000) + 1000}"

def is_pairing_enabled():
    global pairing_enabled, pairing_expiry
    if not pairing_enabled:
        return False
    if time.time() > pairing_expiry:
        pairing_enabled = False
        return False
    return True

load_devices()

class EnhancedProxyHandler(BaseHTTPRequestHandler):
    def log_message(self, format, *args):
        print(f"[{self.log_date_time_string()}] {format % args}")
    
    def send_json(self, code, data):
        response = json.dumps(data, indent=2).encode()
        self.send_response(code)
        self.send_header('Content-Type', 'application/json')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Headers', 'Content-Type, Authorization')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Methods', 'GET, POST, OPTIONS')
        self.end_headers()
        self.wfile.write(response)
    
    def get_client_ip(self):
        return self.client_address[0]
    
    def authenticate(self):
        """Check Bearer token authentication"""
        auth_header = self.headers.get('Authorization', '')
        if not auth_header.startswith('Bearer '):
            return None
        
        token = auth_header[7:].strip()
        token_hash = hash_token(token)
        
        # Find device with this token
        for device_id, device_data in devices.items():
            if device_data.get('token_hash') == token_hash:
                # Update last seen
                device_data['last_seen'] = int(time.time() * 1000)
                save_devices()
                return device_data
        
        return None
    
    def do_OPTIONS(self):
        self.send_response(200)
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Origin', '*')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Methods', 'GET, POST, OPTIONS')
        self.send_header('Access-Control-Allow-Headers', 'Content-Type, Authorization')
        self.end_headers()
    
    def do_GET(self):
        # Health check - no auth required
        if self.path == '/health' or self.path == '/api/v1/health':
            try:
                response = requests.get(f"{LLAMAFILE_URL}/health", timeout=2)
                if response.status_code == 200:
                    self.send_json(200, {
                        "success": True,
                        "data": {
                            "status": "healthy",
                            "backends": "termux,llama",
                            "executor": "file-based"
                        }
                    })
                else:
                    self.send_json(503, {
                        "success": False,
                        "error": "Backend unhealthy"
                    })
            except:
                self.send_json(503, {
                    "success": False,
                    "error": "Backend unreachable"
                })
        
        # Device list - requires auth
        elif self.path == '/devices' or self.path == '/api/v1/devices':
            device = self.authenticate()
            if not device:
                self.send_json(401, {
                    "success": False,
                    "error": "Unauthorized"
                })
                return
            
            device_list = [
                {
                    "id": did,
                    "name": d.get("name", "Unknown"),
                    "ip": d.get("ip", "Unknown"),
                    "paired_at": d.get("paired_at", 0),
                    "last_seen": d.get("last_seen", 0)
                }
                for did, d in devices.items()
            ]
            
            self.send_json(200, {
                "success": True,
                "data": {"devices": device_list}
            })
        else:
            self.send_json(404, {"success": False, "error": "Not found"})
    
    def do_POST(self):
        try:
            content_length = int(self.headers.get('Content-Length', 0))
            body = self.rfile.read(content_length) if content_length > 0 else b'{}'
            data = json.loads(body.decode())
            
            # ======= PAIRING ENDPOINT (NO AUTH) =======
            if self.path == '/pair' or self.path == '/api/v1/pair':
                if not is_pairing_enabled():
                    self.send_json(403, {
                        "success": False,
                        "error": "Pairing mode disabled."
                    })
                    return
                
                device_name = data.get('device_name', '').strip()
                if not device_name:
                    self.send_json(400, {
                        "success": False,
                        "error": "Missing device_name"
                    })
                    return
                
                # Generate credentials
                device_id = generate_device_id()
                token = generate_token()
                token_hash = hash_token(token)
                
                # Save device
                devices[device_id] = {
                    "name": device_name,
                    "token_hash": token_hash,
                    "ip": self.get_client_ip(),
                    "paired_at": int(time.time() * 1000),
                    "last_seen": int(time.time() * 1000)
                }
                save_devices()
                
                print(f"\n✅ Device paired: {device_name} ({device_id})")
                
                self.send_json(200, {
                    "success": True,
                    "data": {
                        "device_id": device_id,
                        "token": token
                    }
                })
                return
            
            # ======= ALL OTHER ENDPOINTS REQUIRE AUTH =======
            device = self.authenticate()
            if not device:
                self.send_json(401, {
                    "success": False,
                    "error": "Unauthorized - missing or invalid token"
                })
                return
            
            # ======= CHAT ENDPOINT =======
            if self.path == '/chat_sync' or self.path == '/chat' or self.path == '/api/v1/chat':
                query = data.get('query', '').strip() or data.get('prompt', '').strip()
                if not query:
                    self.send_json(400, {"success": False, "error": "Missing query"})
                    return
                
                print(f"\n[CHAT] {device.get('name')}: {query}")
                
                response = requests.post(
                    f"{LLAMAFILE_URL}/v1/chat/completions",
                    json={
                        "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": query}],
                        "max_tokens": 100,
                        "temperature": 0.7
                    },
                    timeout=30
                )
                
                if response.status_code != 200:
                    self.send_json(500, {"success": False, "error": "LLM error"})
                    return
                
                result = response.json()
                text = result['choices'][0]['message']['content']
                print(f"[RESPONSE] {text[:100]}...")
                
                self.send_json(200, {"success": True, "data": {"response": text}})
            
            # ======= COMMAND GENERATION =======
            elif self.path == '/generate_sync' or self.path == '/generate' or self.path == '/api/v1/generate':
                query = data.get('query', '').strip() or data.get('prompt', '').strip()
                if not query:
                    self.send_json(400, {"success": False, "error": "Missing query"})
                    return
                
                print(f"\n[GENERATE] {device.get('name')}: {query}")
                
                prompt = f"""Generate a Termux/Android shell command for: {query}

Requirements:
- Single line command only
- Use Termux-compatible syntax
- No placeholders or variables
- Use termux-* commands when appropriate
- Output ONLY the command

Command:"""
                
                response = requests.post(
                    f"{LLAMAFILE_URL}/v1/chat/completions",
                    json={
                        "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
                        "max_tokens": 50,
                        "temperature": 0.3,
                        "stop": ["\n"]
                    },
                    timeout=30
                )
                
                if response.status_code != 200:
                    self.send_json(500, {"success": False, "error": "LLM error"})
                    return
                
                result = response.json()
                command = result['choices'][0]['message']['content'].strip().strip('`"\'')
                
                print(f"[COMMAND] {command}")
                
                self.send_json(200, {
                    "success": True,
                    "data": {
                        "command": command,
                        "response": command
                    }
                })
            
            # ======= COMMAND EXECUTION =======
            elif self.path == '/execute' or self.path == '/api/v1/execute':
                command = data.get('command', '').strip()
                if not command:
                    self.send_json(400, {"success": False, "error": "Missing command"})
                    return
                
                print(f"\n[EXECUTE] {device.get('name')}: {command}")
                
                try:
                    result = subprocess.run(
                        command,
                        shell=True,
                        capture_output=True,
                        text=True,
                        timeout=30,
                        cwd=str(Path.home())
                    )
                    
                    output = result.stdout + result.stderr
                    success = result.returncode == 0
                    
                    print(f"[EXIT CODE] {result.returncode}")
                    
                    self.send_json(200, {
                        "success": success,
                        "data": {
                            "output": output if output else "Command executed (no output)",
                            "exit_code": result.returncode
                        }
                    })
                    
                except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
                    self.send_json(500, {
                        "success": False,
                        "error": "Command timeout (>30s)"
                    })
                except Exception as e:
                    self.send_json(500, {
                        "success": False,
                        "error": f"Execution failed: {e}"
                    })
            
            else:
                self.send_json(404, {"success": False, "error": "Endpoint not found"})
                
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[ERROR] {e}")
            import traceback
            traceback.print_exc()
            self.send_json(500, {"success": False, "error": str(e)})

def enable_pairing(duration_seconds=60):
    global pairing_enabled, pairing_expiry
    pairing_enabled = True
    pairing_expiry = time.time() + duration_seconds
    print(f"\n🔓 PAIRING MODE ENABLED for {duration_seconds} seconds")
    print(f"   Expires at: {datetime.fromtimestamp(pairing_expiry).strftime('%H:%M:%S')}")
    print(f"   Clients can pair to: http://<this-ip>:{PORT}/api/v1/pair")
    print()

if __name__ == '__main__':
    print("="*70)
    print("🤖 JARVIS PROXY SERVER - LAN ENABLED")
    print("="*70)
    print(f"Port: {PORT}")
    print(f"Backend: {LLAMAFILE_URL}")
    print(f"Queue: {QUEUE_DIR}")
    print(f"Devices: {len(devices)} paired")
    print()
    print("Features:")
    print("  ✅ LAN device pairing")
    print("  ✅ Token authentication")
    print("  ✅ Command execution")
    print("  ✅ AI chat & generation")
    print()
    print("Endpoints:")
    print("  GET  /health              - Health check")
    print("  POST /pair                - Pair new device (pairing mode)")
    print("  GET  /devices             - List devices (auth)")
    print("  POST /chat                - AI chat (auth)")
    print("  POST /generate            - Generate command (auth)")
    print("  POST /execute             - Execute command (auth)")
    print("="*70)
    print()
    print("⚠️  PAIRING IS DISABLED BY DEFAULT")
    print("    To enable pairing, press Ctrl+C then restart with --pair flag")
    print("    Or call: enable_pairing() from Python")
    print()
    
    # Check for --pair flag
    import sys
    if '--pair' in sys.argv:
        duration = 300  # 5 minutes default
        if '--duration' in sys.argv:
            idx = sys.argv.index('--duration')
            duration = int(sys.argv[idx + 1])
        enable_pairing(duration)
    
    server = HTTPServer(('0.0.0.0', PORT), EnhancedProxyHandler)
    
    try:
        print(f"🚀 Server listening on 0.0.0.0:{PORT}")
        print(f"   Access from LAN: http://<this-device-ip>:{PORT}")
        print()
        server.serve_forever()
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        print("\n🛑 Shutting down...")
        server.shutdown()


//===== TERMUXFILE: test/extract_ai_output.sh =====
#!/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin/bash
# Extract all files from ai-output.txt
# Usage: bash ~/extract_ai_output.sh [/path/to/ai-output.txt]
INPUT="${1:-$HOME/ai-output.txt}"
BASE="$HOME"
[ -f "$INPUT" ] || { echo "Not found: $INPUT"; exit 1; }
echo "Extracting: $INPUT"
current_file=""; current_content=""; count=0
while IFS= read -r line || [ -n "$line" ]; do
    if [[ "$line" =~ ^=====\ FILE:\ (.+)\ =====$ ]]; then
        if [ -n "$current_file" ] && [ -n "$current_content" ]; then
            dest="$BASE/$current_file"
            mkdir -p "$(dirname "$dest")"
            printf '%s\n' "$current_content" > "$dest"
            [[ "$dest" == *.sh ]] && chmod +x "$dest"
            echo "  ✓ $current_file"; count=$((count+1))
        fi
        current_file="${BASH_REMATCH[1]}"; current_content=""
    elif [ -n "$current_file" ]; then
        [ -z "$current_content" ] && current_content="$line" \
            || current_content="$current_content"$'\n'"$line"
    fi
done < "$INPUT"
if [ -n "$current_file" ] && [ -n "$current_content" ]; then
    dest="$BASE/$current_file"; mkdir -p "$(dirname "$dest")"
    printf '%s\n' "$current_content" > "$dest"
    [[ "$dest" == *.sh ]] && chmod +x "$dest"
    echo "  ✓ $current_file"; count=$((count+1))
fi
echo ""
echo "Extracted $count files."
echo ""
echo "Start system:"
echo "  bash ~/jarvis_server_init.sh"
echo "  bash ~/jarvis_executor.sh &"
echo "  cd ~/jarvis-agent && python3 agent/controller.py"


//===== TERMUXFILE: test/set_ports.py =====
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
set_ports.py — JarvisMinI Port Configuration Tool
Run on either Phone A or Phone B — patches all relevant files.

Usage:
  python3 ~/set_ports.py
"""

import os
import re
import sys

HOME = os.path.expanduser("~")

# ── ANSI colors ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
R   = "\033[1;31m"
G   = "\033[1;32m"
Y   = "\033[1;33m"
B   = "\033[1;34m"
C   = "\033[1;36m"
W   = "\033[1;37m"
DIM = "\033[2m"
RST = "\033[0m"
LINE = f"{DIM}{'─'*54}{RST}"

# ── Files to patch ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# (relative_path, [(label, pattern, replacement)])
# {A_IP}, {A_PORT}, {B_IP}, {B_PORT} substituted at apply time

PATCHES = [
    # Phone B bridge
    ("claude_bridge.py", [
        ("SERIAL",
         r'(SERIAL\s*=\s*")[^"]+(")',
         r'\g<1>{B_IP}:{B_PORT}\g<2>'),
    ]),
    # Phone A agent controller
    ("test/jarvis-agent/agent/controller.py", [
        ("DEFAULT_DEVICE",
         r'(DEFAULT_DEVICE\s*=\s*")[^"]+(")',
         r'\g<1>{A_IP}:{A_PORT}\g<2>'),
    ]),
    ("workflows/test/jarvis-agent/agent/controller.py", [
        ("DEFAULT_DEVICE",
         r'(DEFAULT_DEVICE\s*=\s*")[^"]+(")',
         r'\g<1>{A_IP}:{A_PORT}\g<2>'),
    ]),
    # llm_client — both Phone A serial and Phone B URL
    ("test/jarvis-agent/reasoning/llm_client.py", [
        ("PHONE_B_URL",
         r'(PHONE_B_URL\s*=\s*"http://)[^/]+(:\d+)(")',
         r'\g<1>{B_IP}:{B_PORT}\g<3>'),
        ("PHONE_A_SERIAL",
         r'(PHONE_A_SERIAL\s*=\s*")[^"]+(")',
         r'\g<1>{A_IP}:{A_PORT}\g<2>'),
    ]),
    ("workflows/test/jarvis-agent/reasoning/llm_client.py", [
        ("PHONE_B_URL",
         r'(PHONE_B_URL\s*=\s*"http://)[^/]+(:\d+)(")',
         r'\g<1>{B_IP}:{B_PORT}\g<3>'),
        ("PHONE_A_SERIAL",
         r'(PHONE_A_SERIAL\s*=\s*")[^"]+(")',
         r'\g<1>{A_IP}:{A_PORT}\g<2>'),
    ]),
    # init scripts
    ("jarvis_server_init.sh", [
        ("Phone A port",
         r'192\.168\.\d+\.\d+:\d+',
         None),  # handled specially
    ]),
    ("workflows/jarvis_server_init.sh", [
        ("Phone A/B ports",
         r'192\.168\.\d+\.\d+:\d+',
         None),  # handled specially
    ]),
]

def banner():
    os.system("clear")
    print(f"""
{C}╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║     JARVIS MINI — PORT CONFIGURATION TOOL           ║
║     Updates all config files in one shot            ║
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝{RST}
""")

def read_current():
    """Read current ports from existing files."""
    a_ip, a_port = "192.168.29.48", "37891"
    b_ip, b_port = "192.168.29.110", "39991"

    bridge = os.path.join(HOME, "claude_bridge.py")
    if os.path.exists(bridge):
        m = re.search(r'SERIAL\s*=\s*"([^":]+):(\d+)"', open(bridge).read())
        if m:
            b_ip, b_port = m.group(1), m.group(2)

    for llm_path in [
        "test/jarvis-agent/reasoning/llm_client.py",
        "workflows/test/jarvis-agent/reasoning/llm_client.py",
    ]:
        full = os.path.join(HOME, llm_path)
        if os.path.exists(full):
            text = open(full).read()
            m = re.search(r'PHONE_A_SERIAL\s*=\s*"([^":]+):(\d+)"', text)
            if m:
                a_ip, a_port = m.group(1), m.group(2)
            m2 = re.search(r'PHONE_B_URL\s*=\s*"http://([^/:]+):(\d+)"', text)
            if m2:
                b_ip, b_port = m2.group(1), m2.group(2)
            break

    return a_ip, a_port, b_ip, b_port

def ask_device(name, color, cur_ip, cur_port):
    print(f"  {color}● {name}{RST}")
    print(f"  {DIM}Current: {cur_ip}:{cur_port}{RST}\n")

    ip_in = input(f"  IP   [{cur_ip}]: ").strip()
    ip = ip_in if ip_in else cur_ip

    port_in = input(f"  Port [{cur_port}]: ").strip()
    if port_in and re.match(r'^\d+$', port_in):
        port = port_in
    else:
        port = cur_port
        if port_in:
            print(f"  {Y}Invalid port — keeping {cur_port}{RST}")

    print()
    return ip, port

def apply_simple(rel, label, pattern, repl, a_ip, a_port, b_ip, b_port):
    full = os.path.join(HOME, rel)
    if not os.path.exists(full):
        return

    text = open(full).read()
    r = repl.replace("{A_IP}", a_ip).replace("{A_PORT}", a_port) \
            .replace("{B_IP}", b_ip).replace("{B_PORT}", b_port)
    new = re.sub(pattern, r, text)

    if new != text:
        open(full, "w").write(new)
        print(f"  {G}✓{RST}  {label:<20} {DIM}{rel}{RST}")
    else:
        print(f"  {DIM}~  {label:<20} no match — {rel}{RST}")

def apply_init_sh(rel, a_ip, a_port, b_ip, b_port):
    """Replace all IP:port pairs in shell scripts mapping old→new."""
    full = os.path.join(HOME, rel)
    if not os.path.exists(full):
        return

    text = open(full).read()
    original = text

    # collect all unique IP:port pairs in file
    pairs = re.findall(r'(192\.168\.\d+\.\d+):(\d+)', text)
    if not pairs:
        print(f"  {DIM}~  no IP:port found — {rel}{RST}")
        return

    # heuristic: lower port → Phone A, higher port or second IP → Phone B
    # just replace all — user controls which is A vs B via prompt
    unique = list(dict.fromkeys(pairs))  # preserve order, dedupe

    if len(unique) >= 2:
        old_a_ip, old_a_port = unique[0]
        old_b_ip, old_b_port = unique[1]
        text = text.replace(f"{old_a_ip}:{old_a_port}", f"{a_ip}:{a_port}")
        text = text.replace(f"{old_b_ip}:{old_b_port}", f"{b_ip}:{b_port}")
    elif len(unique) == 1:
        old_ip, old_port = unique[0]
        text = text.replace(f"{old_ip}:{old_port}", f"{b_ip}:{b_port}")

    if text != original:
        open(full, "w").write(text)
        print(f"  {G}✓{RST}  ports updated      {DIM}{rel}{RST}")
    else:
        print(f"  {DIM}~  no changes        {rel}{RST}")

def confirm(a_ip, a_port, b_ip, b_port):
    print(LINE)
    print(f"\n  {W}Summary:{RST}\n")
    print(f"  {B}Phone A (OPPO){RST}              {a_ip}:{a_port}")
    print(f"  {C}Phone B (Galaxy A10s){RST}       {b_ip}:{b_port}")
    print()
    ans = input(f"  Apply? [{G}Y{RST}/{R}n{RST}]: ").strip().lower()
    return ans in ("", "y", "yes")

def main():
    banner()

    a_ip, a_port, b_ip, b_port = read_current()

    print(f"  {W}Current:{RST}")
    print(f"  {B}Phone A{RST}  {a_ip}:{a_port}")
    print(f"  {C}Phone B{RST}  {b_ip}:{b_port}")
    print(f"\n{LINE}\n")
    print(f"  Press {G}Enter{RST} to keep current value\n")

    print(f"{B}  PHONE A — OPPO (agent loop){RST}")
    a_ip, a_port = ask_device("Phone A", B, a_ip, a_port)

    print(LINE)
    print()

    print(f"{C}  PHONE B — Samsung Galaxy A10s (bridge){RST}")
    b_ip, b_port = ask_device("Phone B", C, b_ip, b_port)

    if not confirm(a_ip, a_port, b_ip, b_port):
        print(f"\n  {Y}Cancelled.{RST}\n")
        sys.exit(0)

    print(f"\n{LINE}")
    print(f"  {W}Applying...{RST}\n")

    for rel, patches in PATCHES:
        for label, pattern, repl in patches:
            if repl is None:
                apply_init_sh(rel, a_ip, a_port, b_ip, b_port)
                break
            else:
                apply_simple(rel, label, pattern, repl, a_ip, a_port, b_ip, b_port)

    print(f"\n{LINE}")
    print(f"\n  {G}Done.{RST}\n")
    print(f"  {DIM}Phone B — restart bridge:{RST}")
    print(f"  pkill -f claude_bridge && python3 ~/claude_bridge.py\n")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()


//===== TERMUXFILE: perception/screen_map.py =====
"""
perception/screen_map.py  —  Screen Understanding + App Navigation Graph

Session 8 fixes:
  - Canonical screen deduplication: filter-tab variants of HomeActivity all
    resolve to one canonical screen_id so the graph stays small and coherent.
  - Unknown-screen filter: screens with package=="unknown" are never registered.
  - Call-overlay guard: screens whose labels include active-call markers
    (Turn microphone off / Leave call / WhatsApp voice call) are recognised as
    a call-overlay variant of their base screen and kept separate but labelled.
  - get_canonical_id(): returns the highest-visit variant for a given activity
    so controller.py and transition_memory.py always use a stable anchor node.

Data stored in ~/workflows/screen_map.json:
  screens:     fingerprinted UI states
  transitions: (screen_id, action) → screen_id edges

Usage:
  from perception.screen_map import ScreenMap
  sm = ScreenMap()
  screen_id = sm.identify(activity, elements)
  path = sm.find_path(start_id, target_id)
"""

import hashlib
import json
import re
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Optional

MAP_FILE = Path.home() / "workflows" / "screen_map.json"

# Elements to ignore when fingerprinting (too dynamic)
_IGNORE_TEXTS = {
    "", "1", "2", "3", "ok", "cancel", "back", "home", "done",
}
_IGNORE_PATTERNS = [
    r"^\d{1,2}:\d{2}(:\d{2})?$",   # timestamps
    r"^\d+$",                        # pure numbers
    r"^[+\-]?\d+[\d.,]*$",          # numbers with decimals
]

# Destructive elements the crawler must never tap
_DANGER_WORDS = {
    "delete", "remove", "block", "unblock", "report", "pay", "purchase",
    "buy", "uninstall", "clear", "reset", "erase", "format", "factory",
    "logout", "sign out", "deactivate", "disable", "turn off",
}

# Labels that signal an active call overlay — screen is "tainted"
_CALL_OVERLAY_LABELS = {
    "turn microphone off",
    "leave call",
    "whatsapp voice call",
    "minimize call",
    "add person to call",
}

# Filter-tab labels in WhatsApp HomeActivity — these make the fingerprint
# differ per tab but the screen is functionally the same home screen.
# Presence of ANY of these does NOT make a new canonical screen.
_HOME_FILTER_LABELS = {
    "all filter, , selected",
    "unread filter, 2, unselected",
    "unread filter, 0, unselected",
    "favourites filter, , unselected",
    "groups filter, , unselected",
    "family filter, , unselected",
    "search unread chats",
    "manage unread",
    "search favourite chats",
    "manage favourites",
    "search group chats",
    "search family",
    "add new list",
    "manage family",
    # Search overlay pills
    "unread", "photos", "videos", "links", "gifs", "audio",
    "documents", "stickers", "polls",
}


def _is_dynamic(text: str) -> bool:
    if text.lower() in _IGNORE_TEXTS:
        return True
    for pat in _IGNORE_PATTERNS:
        if re.match(pat, text.strip()):
            return True
    return False


def _is_dangerous(text: str) -> bool:
    tl = text.lower()
    return any(w in tl for w in _DANGER_WORDS)


def _has_call_overlay(labels: list) -> bool:
    """Return True if any call-overlay label is present in label list."""
    low = {l.lower() for l in labels}
    return any(cl in " ".join(low) for cl in _CALL_OVERLAY_LABELS)


def _strip_filter_labels(labels: list) -> list:
    """Remove filter-tab / search-overlay labels before fingerprinting."""
    return [l for l in labels if l.lower() not in _HOME_FILTER_LABELS]


class ScreenMap:
    """
    Stores screen fingerprints and navigation graph.

    Screen fingerprint:
      screen_id = md5(package + "/" + activity_tail + "|" + sorted_stable_labels)

    Navigation graph:
      transitions[(screen_id, element_text)] = target_screen_id
    """

    def __init__(self):
        self._data = self._load()

    # -- Persistence -----------------------------------------------------------

    def _load(self) -> dict:
        if MAP_FILE.exists():
            try:
                return json.loads(MAP_FILE.read_text())
            except Exception:
                pass
        return {"screens": {}, "transitions": {}}

    def _save(self):
        MAP_FILE.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        MAP_FILE.write_text(json.dumps(self._data, indent=2))

    # -- Fingerprinting --------------------------------------------------------

    @staticmethod
    def fingerprint(activity: str, elements: list) -> str:
        """
        Stable hash for a screen state.
        Filter-tab variants of HomeActivity collapse to one fingerprint.
        Call overlays get their own fingerprint (tainted screen).
        """
        pkg      = activity.split("/")[0] if "/" in activity else activity
        act_tail = activity.split("/")[-1].split(".")[-1]

        raw_labels = [
            e.get("text", "") for e in elements
            if e.get("text", "") and not _is_dynamic(e.get("text", ""))
        ]

        # For HomeActivity, strip filter/search labels before hashing
        if "HomeActivity" in act_tail or "homeactivity" in act_tail.lower():
            labels = _strip_filter_labels(raw_labels)
        else:
            labels = raw_labels

        labels_sorted = sorted(set(labels))
        blob = f"{pkg}/{act_tail}|{'|'.join(labels_sorted[:20])}"
        return hashlib.md5(blob.encode()).hexdigest()[:12]

    @staticmethod
    def similarity(labels_a: list, labels_b: list) -> float:
        """Overlap ratio between two element label sets."""
        a = {t for t in labels_a if t and not _is_dynamic(t)}
        b = {t for t in labels_b if t and not _is_dynamic(t)}
        if not b:
            return 0.0
        return len(a & b) / len(b)

    # -- Screen registry -------------------------------------------------------

    def identify(self, activity: str, elements: list) -> Optional[str]:
        """
        Return screen_id for the current state.
        Returns None for screens with unknown package (loading screens etc.)
        Call-overlay screens are registered but labelled as tainted.
        """
        # Reject loading / transition screens
        pkg = activity.split("/")[0] if "/" in activity else activity
        if pkg in ("unknown", "") or not pkg:
            return None

        fp = self.fingerprint(activity, elements)
        screens = self._data["screens"]

        if fp in screens:
            screens[fp]["visits"] = screens[fp].get("visits", 0) + 1
            self._save()
            return fp

        # New screen — register it
        act_tail = activity.split("/")[-1].split(".")[-1]
        labels   = [
            e.get("text", "") for e in elements
            if e.get("text", "") and not _is_dynamic(e.get("text", ""))
        ]

        tainted = _has_call_overlay(labels)
        name    = f"{pkg.split('.')[-1]}_{act_tail}".lower()
        if tainted:
            name += "_call_overlay"

        screens[fp] = {
            "screen_id":     fp,
            "package":       pkg,
            "activity":      activity,
            "name":          name,
            "labels":        labels[:30],
            "visits":        1,
            "tainted":       tainted,
            "elements":      [
                {k: v for k, v in e.items()
                 if k in ("text", "resource_id", "cls", "x", "y")}
                for e in elements[:40]
            ],
        }
        self._save()
        flag = " [CALL OVERLAY]" if tainted else ""
        print(f"[map] new screen: {name} ({fp}){flag}")
        return fp

    def get_screen(self, screen_id: str) -> Optional[dict]:
        return self._data["screens"].get(screen_id)

    def get_canonical_id(self, activity: str) -> Optional[str]:
        """
        Return the screen_id with the most visits for a given activity string.
        Used by controller to get a stable anchor when multiple fingerprint
        variants exist for the same activity (e.g. WhatsApp home w/ filter tabs).
        Ignores tainted (call-overlay) screens.
        """
        best_id, best_visits = None, -1
        for sid, s in self._data["screens"].items():
            if s.get("activity", "") != activity:
                continue
            if s.get("tainted", False):
                continue
            v = s.get("visits", 0)
            if v > best_visits:
                best_visits = v
                best_id = sid
        return best_id

    def find_by_name(self, name: str) -> Optional[str]:
        """Find screen_id by partial name match. Returns highest-visit match."""
        name_l = name.lower()
        best_id, best_visits = None, -1
        for sid, s in self._data["screens"].items():
            if s.get("tainted", False):
                continue
            if name_l in s.get("name", "").lower():
                v = s.get("visits", 0)
                if v > best_visits:
                    best_visits = v
                    best_id = sid
        return best_id

    def find_by_labels(self, labels: list, threshold=0.6) -> Optional[str]:
        """Find screen_id by element label similarity. Ignores tainted screens."""
        best_id, best_score = None, 0.0
        for sid, s in self._data["screens"].items():
            if s.get("tainted", False):
                continue
            score = self.similarity(labels, s.get("labels", []))
            if score > best_score:
                best_score = score
                best_id = sid
        if best_score >= threshold:
            return best_id
        return None

    # -- Navigation graph ------------------------------------------------------

    def record_transition(self, from_id: str, action_label: str, to_id: str):
        """
        Record a (screen, action) → screen edge.
        Skips transitions involving tainted (call-overlay) screens.
        """
        if from_id == to_id:
            return
        if from_id is None or to_id is None:
            return

        from_screen = self._data["screens"].get(from_id, {})
        to_screen   = self._data["screens"].get(to_id, {})
        if from_screen.get("tainted") or to_screen.get("tainted"):
            return  # don't record call-overlay transitions

        key = f"{from_id}|{action_label}"
        transitions = self._data["transitions"]
        if transitions.get(key) != to_id:
            transitions[key] = to_id
            self._save()
            from_name = from_screen.get("name", from_id[:8])
            to_name   = to_screen.get("name",   to_id[:8])
            print(f"[map] transition: {from_name} --[{action_label}]--> {to_name}")

    def find_path(self, from_id: str, to_id: str, max_depth=8) -> Optional[list]:
        """
        BFS over transition graph to find action sequence from_id → to_id.
        Returns list of (action_label, screen_id) tuples or None.
        """
        if from_id == to_id:
            return []
        if from_id is None or to_id is None:
            return None

        transitions = self._data["transitions"]
        adj = {}
        for key, target in transitions.items():
            src, action = key.rsplit("|", 1)
            adj.setdefault(src, []).append((action, target))

        queue   = [(from_id, [])]
        visited = {from_id}
        while queue:
            curr, path = queue.pop(0)
            if len(path) >= max_depth:
                continue
            for action, nxt in adj.get(curr, []):
                if nxt in visited:
                    continue
                new_path = path + [(action, nxt)]
                if nxt == to_id:
                    return new_path
                visited.add(nxt)
                queue.append((nxt, new_path))
        return None

    # -- Stats -----------------------------------------------------------------

    def stats(self) -> dict:
        screens     = self._data["screens"]
        transitions = self._data["transitions"]
        by_pkg = {}
        tainted_count = 0
        for s in screens.values():
            pkg = s.get("package", "?")
            by_pkg[pkg] = by_pkg.get(pkg, 0) + 1
            if s.get("tainted"):
                tainted_count += 1
        return {
            "total_screens":     len(screens),
            "tainted_screens":   tainted_count,
            "total_transitions": len(transitions),
            "by_package":        by_pkg,
        }

    def print_stats(self):
        st = self.stats()
        print(f"\n  Screen Map: {st['total_screens']} screens "
              f"({st['tainted_screens']} tainted), "
              f"{st['total_transitions']} transitions")
        for pkg, count in sorted(st["by_package"].items(),
                                  key=lambda x: -x[1]):
            print(f"    {pkg.split('.')[-1]:<20} {count} screens")


//===== TERMUXFILE: perception/transition_memory.py =====
"""
perception/transition_memory.py  —  OPT 7: UI Transition Prediction

Eliminates the perception wait after known actions by predicting the next
screen before the dump is complete.

How it works:
  After every action is executed, record_transition() stores:
    (current_screen_id, action_description) -> expected_next_screen_id

  Before the next perception step, get_predicted_screen() returns the
  expected next screen if the action is known. The controller can then:
    1. Skip the full UI dump if the predicted screen is cached in ScreenMemory
    2. Return the cached UI immediately (~0ms vs 900ms)
    3. If prediction is wrong (actual != predicted), record the correction

Integration in controller.py run_step():
  BEFORE parse_ui():
    predicted = tm.get_predicted_screen(current_screen_id, last_action_label)
    if predicted:
        ui = screen_memory.get_by_screen_id(predicted)
        if ui: ... use cached UI ...

  AFTER action executes:
    tm.record(current_screen_id, action_label, new_screen_id)

Data stored in ~/workflows/transition_memory.json

Timing impact (from report targets):
  Without prediction: 3.7s/step   (dump + parse + wait)
  With prediction:    2.0s/step   (cache hit → no dump)
  Novel steps still take full 3.7s (first time on a transition)
"""

import json
import time
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Optional

TM_FILE = Path.home() / "workflows" / "transition_memory.json"

# How many seconds to wait before giving up on a predicted transition
PREDICTION_TIMEOUT = 3.0

# Minimum times a transition must be observed before we trust the prediction
MIN_OBSERVATIONS = 2


class TransitionMemory:
    """
    Stores observed (screen_id, action) -> screen_id transitions
    with confidence counts.

    Keys:   "{from_screen_id}|{action_label}"
    Values: {"to": screen_id, "count": int, "last_seen": float}
    """

    def __init__(self):
        self._data = self._load()
        self._pending: Optional[tuple] = None   # (from_id, action_label, t_start)

    # -- Persistence -----------------------------------------------------------

    def _load(self) -> dict:
        if TM_FILE.exists():
            try:
                return json.loads(TM_FILE.read_text())
            except Exception:
                pass
        return {}

    def _save(self):
        TM_FILE.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        TM_FILE.write_text(json.dumps(self._data, indent=2))

    # -- Recording -------------------------------------------------------------

    def record(self, from_id: str, action_label: str, to_id: str):
        """
        Record an observed transition.
        Called after every action executes and the new screen is identified.
        """
        if not from_id or not to_id or from_id == to_id:
            return

        key = f"{from_id}|{action_label}"
        entry = self._data.get(key)

        if entry and entry.get("to") == to_id:
            # Same destination — increment confidence
            entry["count"]     = entry.get("count", 1) + 1
            entry["last_seen"] = time.time()
        else:
            # New or changed destination — reset with count=1
            if entry and entry.get("to") != to_id:
                print(f"[tm] transition changed: {key[:40]} "
                      f"{entry['to'][:8]} -> {to_id[:8]}")
            self._data[key] = {
                "to":        to_id,
                "count":     1,
                "last_seen": time.time(),
            }

        self._save()

    def set_pending(self, from_id: str, action_label: str):
        """
        Mark that we just executed an action and are waiting for the new screen.
        Call this immediately after the action executes, before the next
        perception step, so the controller can time the transition wait.
        """
        self._pending = (from_id, action_label, time.time())

    def clear_pending(self):
        self._pending = None

    # -- Prediction ------------------------------------------------------------

    def get_predicted_screen(self, from_id: str, action_label: str) -> Optional[str]:
        """
        Return predicted next screen_id if transition is known with sufficient
        confidence, or None if unknown / low confidence.

        Only returns predictions with MIN_OBSERVATIONS or more observations.
        """
        if not from_id or not action_label:
            return None

        key   = f"{from_id}|{action_label}"
        entry = self._data.get(key)
        if not entry:
            return None

        if entry.get("count", 0) < MIN_OBSERVATIONS:
            return None

        return entry["to"]

    def get_pending_prediction(self) -> Optional[str]:
        """
        If set_pending() was called, return the predicted next screen for the
        pending action. Returns None if no pending action or prediction unknown.
        """
        if not self._pending:
            return None
        from_id, action_label, _ = self._pending
        return self.get_predicted_screen(from_id, action_label)

    def pending_elapsed(self) -> float:
        """Seconds since set_pending() was called."""
        if not self._pending:
            return 0.0
        return time.time() - self._pending[2]

    # -- Batch seeding ---------------------------------------------------------

    def seed_from_screen_map(self, screen_map_data: dict):
        """
        Pre-populate TransitionMemory from an existing screen_map.json.
        Uses count=MIN_OBSERVATIONS so seeded transitions are immediately trusted.

        Call once after a crawl completes to bootstrap predictions.

        Usage:
            import json
            from pathlib import Path
            from perception.transition_memory import TransitionMemory

            sm_data = json.loads((Path.home()/"workflows"/"screen_map.json").read_text())
            tm = TransitionMemory()
            tm.seed_from_screen_map(sm_data)
        """
        transitions = screen_map_data.get("transitions", {})
        screens     = screen_map_data.get("screens", {})
        seeded = 0

        for key, to_id in transitions.items():
            # Skip transitions involving tainted screens
            to_screen = screens.get(to_id, {})
            if to_screen.get("tainted"):
                continue

            from_id = key.split("|")[0]
            from_screen = screens.get(from_id, {})
            if from_screen.get("tainted"):
                continue

            # Only seed if not already known
            if key not in self._data:
                self._data[key] = {
                    "to":        to_id,
                    "count":     MIN_OBSERVATIONS,
                    "last_seen": time.time(),
                    "seeded":    True,
                }
                seeded += 1

        if seeded:
            self._save()
            print(f"[tm] seeded {seeded} transitions from screen_map")

    # -- Stats -----------------------------------------------------------------

    def stats(self) -> dict:
        total     = len(self._data)
        confirmed = sum(1 for e in self._data.values()
                        if e.get("count", 0) >= MIN_OBSERVATIONS)
        return {
            "total_transitions": total,
            "confirmed":         confirmed,
            "pending":           self._pending is not None,
        }

    def print_stats(self):
        st = self.stats()
        print(f"  TransitionMemory: {st['total_transitions']} transitions "
              f"({st['confirmed']} confirmed, threshold={MIN_OBSERVATIONS})")
